***kansel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kansel.html>kansel</a> (45274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kanzel</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">kanzel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">cancella</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:late.html>Late</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cancellī</i>, plural <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cancellus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kansel.html>kansel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kansel.html>kansels</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kansel.html>kanseltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:karakter.html>karakter</a> (3141)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">caracter</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:character.html>character</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χαρακτήρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kharaktḗr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:karakter.html>karakter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:karakters.html>karakters</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:karakter.html>karaktertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:karig.html>karig</a> (45269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*karag</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*karagaz</i>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">karg</i>.

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">carrosse</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">carrozza</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:derivation.html>derivation</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">carro</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carrus</i>. Doublet <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kar.html>kar</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:karper.html>karper</a> (29869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Plausibly <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:vulgar.html>Vulgar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carpa</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:unknown.html>unknown</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:origin.html>origin</a>; cognates <a href = vnd.unilang:include.html>include</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:carp.html>carp</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:carpe.html>carpe</a>, Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">карп</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:karp.html>karp</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Serbo-Croatian kräp, kárpa, Italian carpione
</p>
